<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:герметический.html>гермети́ческий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">germetíčeskij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>hermetic (not letting gas or water through, waterproof or gasproof)</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>гер<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ме<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ти.html>ти́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>чес<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:кий.html>кий</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:относительный.html>относи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 3a✕~.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-гермет-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ическ</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ий</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:герметичный.html>гермети́чный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">germetíčnyj</span>)

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἡρωΐνη</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">hērōḯnē</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, with the ending influenced by the feminine suffix <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ы́ня</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ýnja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:героиня.html>герои́ня</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">geroínja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:героиня.html>герои́ни</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:героиня.html>герои́ни</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:героиня.html>герои́нь</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:герой.html>геро́й</a> (603)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">héros</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">hērōs</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἥρως</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">hḗrōs</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">demi-god, hero</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Influenced by the displaced earlier <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">иро́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">irój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, directly from the Greek. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">hero</i>.
</p>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:герой.html>геро́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gerój</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:герой.html>геро́я</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:герой.html>геро́и</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:герой.html>геро́ев</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:героиня.html>герои́ня</a></b>)

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literature</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> character, protagonist</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:геройский.html>геро́йский</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gerójskij</span>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:герцогиня.html>герцоги́ня</a> (25416)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Herzogin</i>, with the ending influenced by the feminine suffix <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ы́ня</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ýnja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:герцогиня.html>герцоги́ня</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gercogínja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:герцогиня.html>герцоги́ни</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:герцогиня.html>герцоги́ни</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:герцогиня.html>герцоги́нь</a></b>, <i>masculine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ге́рцог</b>)
</p>

<p><b>гер<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>цо<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ги́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ня</b>

***гибель.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:гибель.html>ги́бель</a> (2469)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">гꙑбель</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gybelĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*gybělь</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*gyb-</i> + |  <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*-ělь</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гибель.html>ги́бель</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gíbelʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гибель.html>ги́бели</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гибель.html>ги́бели</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гибель.html>ги́белей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>loss, death</li>
<li>destruction, ruin</li>
<li>lots of, immense number</li></ol>

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:гибельный.html>ги́бельная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:политика.html>поли́тика</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>gíbelʹnaja</b> polítika</i> ― <span class="e-translation">ruinous/disastrous policy</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>fatal</li></ol>
